# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="eff64-103">Catene di crittografia di Microsoft 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eff64-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eff64-104">Microsoft 365 sfrutta diversi provider di certificati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eff64-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eff64-105">Di seguito viene descritto l'elenco completo dei certificati radice di Microsoft 365 noti che i clienti possono riscontrare quando accedono a Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eff64-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eff64-106">Per informazioni sui certificati che potrebbe essere necessario installare nella propria infrastruttura, vedere [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eff64-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eff64-107">Le seguenti informazioni sui certificati si applicano a tutte le istanze cloud nazionali e internazionali di Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eff64-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>
